---
title: Bill Line Items Fact Table
excerpt: ''
deprecated: false
hidden: false
metadata:
  title: ''
  description: ''
  robots: index
next:
  description: ''
---
The Bill Line Items fact table provides a granular level view of each transaction at the line item level. For instance, if a customer buys 5 items in a single transaction, the table would contain 5 rows corresponding to each line item. This table captures the information such as bill amount, discount, GST details, line item description, quantity, and price.

**Databricks Table Name:** bill\_lineitems

<Note title="Note">
Bill level details remain the same and are repeated across rows.
</Note>

**Bill Line Items - Entity Relationship Diagram (ERD)**

Zoom in the table for more clarity. Click the table title to view its details.

**Bill Line Items Facts Table**

  <tbody>
    <tr>
      <td>
        allocated\_points
      </td>

      <td>
        double
      </td>

      <td>
        Number of loyalty points allocated to a customer for a specific transaction. Can be on bill level, line item level or customer level.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Allocated Points
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        additional\_discount
      </td>

      <td>
        double
      </td>

      <td>
        Extra discount availed on a transaction, for example, discount on combo or bulk items. However, this is a extended field and takes the user input values.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Additional Discount
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        auto\_update\_time\_bill
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Date and time when the corresponding record in the bill table available at the source was last updated. It is in the Unix timestamp format.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Auto Update Time Bill
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        auto\_update\_time\_combo\_details
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Date and time when the corresponding record in the combo\_details table available at the source was last updated. Combos typically refer to bundled offers or packages where multiple items are sold together at a discounted price. It is in the Unix timestamp format.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Auto Update Time Combo Details
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        auto\_update\_time\_lineitem
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>

      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Auto Update Time Lineitem
      </td>
    </tr>

        reason
      </td>

      <td>
        string
      </td>

      <td>
        Captures the reason for the transaction.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Reason
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        redeemed\_points
      </td>

      <td>
        double
      </td>

      <td>
        Points redeemed on the bill level.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Redeemed Points
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        state\_gst
      </td>

      <td>
        double
      </td>

      <td>
        Taxes levied by the State Government on the bill.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Lineitem State Gst
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        tax\_amount
      </td>

      <td>
        double
      </td>

      <td>
        Total amount of tax levied on the bill.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Tax Amount
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        total\_quantity
      </td>

      <td>
        integer
      </td>

      <td>
        Total number of line items in the bill.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Total Quantity
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        total\_unit\_cost
      </td>

      <td>
        double
      </td>

      <td>
        Total price of the item including tax and other charges
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Total Unit Cost
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        visit\_count
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Total number of visits made by a customer. It is based on the number of transactions recorded for the customer.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Visit Count
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        visit\_day\_count
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Total number of visits made by a customer based on dates. Even if the customer visits multiple times on a particular day, it will only count as one day in the visit count.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Measure Name: Visit Day Count
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        year
      </td>

      <td>
        integer
      </td>

      <td>
        Year when the transaction was done.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Year
      </td>
    </tr>

    <tr>
      <td>
        dim\_membership\_id
      </td>

      <td>
        bigint
      </td>

      <td>
        Membership type of the customer who completed the transaction. Possible values are - member/ not interested/ loyalty-not-interested. It is the primary key of the Bill\_Lineitems facts table.
      </td>

      <td>
        \_
      </td>

      <td>
        Yes; Dimension Name: Membership > Id
      </td>
    </tr>
  </tbody>
</Table>
